The President @fhollande has just arrived in Santiago de Chile for an official visit at the invitation of @mbachelet https://t.co/fzPxcxc0lN
The two heads of state will launch the Franco-Chilean year of innovation. France is one of Chile's leading scientific partners.
A @LaFrenchTech community was created in Santiago in 2016. @fhollande will also visit the site of the EDF Bolero solar power plant.
On the economic front, the bilateral relationship is dense: 250 French companies are in Chile and employ about 50,000 people.
During the 1970s and 1980s, France hosted more than 10,000 Chilean refugees. There will be an important memory dimension
The links between France and Chile are historically strong and marked by the history of the country.
President @fhollande is on an official visit to Chile for 2 days. This is the first visit of a French head of state since 2006
